CHAPTER 3
It was half past 9 and David tried to sleep in his bed. He shut his eyes hard and tried to drift away into the realm of dreams leaving the painful reality behind .But something kept pulling him. He sat up broken without knowing what to do. Like a boon from the god, his mother called him. Over joyed he cried on hearing her voice and his masculine voice turned into a fog of whisper, whispering â€œma! I miss you!, please come and save your little child.â€
Upset over hearing her son cry, she asked â€œwhat is it thatâ€™s bothering my baby?? Did someone bully you at work??â€

â€œNo ma!...â€ cried David as heated tears roll down his cheeks. â€œTerrible things are happening to me ma! â€œ
â€œDonâ€™t worry baby! Itâ€™s going to be fine. Come over to my placeâ€ said his mom, trying to reassure him.

Usually it was a 2 hr drive from his home, to his momsâ€™ place. But today it took longer than usual. There was no public transport as rain clogged each nuke end corner of the city. 1/21/22, 10:59â€¯PM - Patrick Jane: I lay on the bed, with my eyes fixed to the ceiling. The slow whirring sound of the air conditioner filled the room. I needed silence so I turned it off. I try to fix my attention on the ceiling again but the moon keeked through the transparent window right at my face. Irritated I got up from the bed and showed my middle finger @ the moon and drew the curtains over the window. I dug my face in the bed and tried hard to level my thoughts. My mind was wavering.
 Slowly my mind calmed down and my muscles relaxed. But all of a sudden an owl sitting on some twig of a tree started hooting loudly. Even through the closed window I could hear it so distinctly. I covered my ears with my pillows so hard till it hurts but as I pressed harder the owl hooted even more loudly. Even more irritated now, I wrapped myself with the blanket and mummified myself. For about 15 minutes the owl hooted at its peak voice. Then slowly the owl stopped hooting. Relieved I slowly unwrapped myself and inhaled a one big mouthful of air and I let it pass down through my oesophogous into my stomach, swirling their way from small intestine to large intestine and out away. I oxygenated my blood. To my left was a digital clock hanging on the wall. What caught my attention was the time was still and seconds refused to proceed further into the future. The clock stopped at 12:07am.
It was the 3rd time in the week the clock stopped working. Thinking what could have possibly gone wrong I scratched my head lying in the bed. The room was unusually chill. I had to smother my body with the blanket to prevent the heat from escaping from my body. I Twisted and turned but I could not sleep. 
Slowly I felt and cold wind being blown into my ears. It was so cold that my ear drums frosted. Panicked I jumped up to see my baby little sister blowing in my ear. She had tied her hair in two sided pony tail and was laughing so cutely that instantly my heart melted. She was holding her favorite Barbie doll. My parents said that she had gone to her grandparentsâ€™ home. Now that she came back I was so happy. I hugged her so hard transferring all my heat to her. She was as cold as an iceberg. We played all night, singing dancing and I read her stories and by 3:00am she was sound asleep in my lap. I put her on the bed and lied down with her and started to sleep. Even when she was sleeping she clutched her doll so tightly with hand and clasped my thumb with her other hand. I instantly slept. 
Next morning I woke up to see my sister gone. Worried I dressed myself and started out early in the morning @ 6am to see whether my sister had reached her place safely. I walked the empty streets clasping my body with my hands. The fog was so low and freezing that I could hardly see. The fog was slowly turning into droplets of ice and was hitting my face so hard. Wiping it away I walked with steady momentum.      I reached the spot. I was so relieved to find that my sister has reached safely. She was sleeping heavily in her coffin clutching her favorite doll. The same doll that we buried with her when she died. What was more terrifying?? The fact that I realized that the clock in my home stopped working  everyday exactly at the time when my sister breathed her last breath or the fact that even after 5 years my parents still visit my grave with a blue face to pay homage. The grave I specially asked for next to my sistersâ€™??
